Widget   thá»i   tiáº¿t   khÃ­   tÆ°á»£ng : Äá»‹nh   ká»³   10   phÃºt   má»™t   láº§n,   luá»“ng   chÃ­nh   gá»i   API   Open-Meteo Ä‘á»ƒ cáº­p nháº­t thÃ´ng tin nhiá»‡t Ä‘á»™, Ä‘á»™ áº©m vÃ  sá»©c giÃ³ thá»±c táº¿ táº¡i khu vá»±c cá»©u há»™ thÃ´ng qua káº¿t ná»‘i Internet, hiá»ƒn thá»‹ trá»±c tiáº¿p lÃªn widget giao diá»‡n. Tinh   toan   PID   Cascade   cho   truc   Roll   (   pid_controller.   cpp) void   pid   Compute   (   const   Attitude   *   current_att   ,   const   Mpu   Data   *  current_imu   , float   target_roll_deg   ,   float   *   out_roll)   { //   Bo   loc   thong   thap   IIR   70/30   lam   muot   tin   hieu   gyro   truoc   khi   tinh   PID gyro_roll_input   =   (   gyro_roll_input   *   0.7   f)   +   (   current_imu   -   > gx   *   0.3   f); //   Vong   ngoai:   Angle   - >   Rate   setpoint float   error_angle_roll   =   target_roll_deg   -   current_att   -   >   roll ; float   target_rate_roll   =   angle_gains   [   AXIS_ROLL   ].   kp   *  error_angle_roll   ; //   Gioi   han   rate   setpoint   o   muc   +- 164   deg/s   de   dam   bao   an   toan if   (   target_rate_roll   >   164.0   f)   target_rate_roll   =   164.0   f;  else   if   (   target_rate_roll   <   - 164.0   f)   target_rate_roll   = - 164.0   f; //    Vong    trong:    Rate    PID float    error_rate_roll    =    gyro_roll_input    -   target_rate_roll   ; //   Khau   tich   phan   (I)   khong   nhan   dt,   co   chong   bao   hoa   (   Anti   -   windup   clamping) i_mem_roll   +=   rate_gains   [   AXIS_ROLL   ].   ki   *   error_rate_roll   ; if   (   pid_output_roll   >   PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   )   pid_output_roll   =  PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   ; else   if   (   pid_output_roll   <   -   PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   )  pid_output_roll   =   -   PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   ; last_error_roll   =    error_rate_roll   ; *   out_roll   =    pid_output_roll   ; } float   pid_output_roll   =   rate_gains   [   AXIS_ROLL   ].   kp   *  error_rate_roll   +   i_mem_roll   + rate_gains[   AXIS_ROLL   ].   kd   *   (  error_rate_roll  -  last_error_roll ); if   (   pid_output_roll   >   PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   )   pid_output_roll   =  PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   ; else   if   (   pid_output_roll   <   -   PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   )  pid_output_roll   =   -   PID_MAX_ROLL_PITCH   ; last_error_roll   =    error_rate_roll   ; *   out_roll   =    pid_output_roll   ; } Phá»¥   lá»¥c   B:   MÃ£   nguá»“n   Python   thuáº­t   toÃ¡n   phÃ¡t   hiá»‡n   cá»­   chá»‰   váº«y   tay   cáº§u   cá»©u #   1.
